        <div data-pjax="true" data-test-selector="body-content" data-view-component="true" class="markdown-body my-3"><h1> Whats New in Mem0 v1.0.0</h1>
<p>This release marks a major milestone for Mem0  introducing <strong>v1.0.0</strong> with key architectural improvements, expanded vector store integrations, and broader LLM provider compatibility. Expect better performance, more stability, and enhanced developer experience across SDKs.</p>
<h2> New Features</h2>
<ul>
<li>Added <strong>Azure MySQL</strong> support for improved cloud database flexibility by <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/parshvadaftari/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/parshvadaftari">@parshvadaftari</a></li>
<li>Introduced <strong>Azure AI Search Vector Store</strong> support for the TypeScript SDK by <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/G26karthik/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/G26karthik">@G26karthik</a></li>
<li>Added <strong>Tool Call support</strong> for LangchainLLM by <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/soapun/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/soapun">@soapun</a></li>
<li>Enabled <strong>custom model and parameters</strong> for Hugging Face with <code>huggingface_base_url</code> by <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/vedant381/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/vedant381">@vedant381</a></li>
<li>Added <strong>default LLM configuration updates</strong> for streamlined setup by <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/parshvadaftari/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/parshvadaftari">@parshvadaftari</a></li>
<li>Enabled <strong>async mode as default</strong> for optimized performance by <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/kk2211/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/kk2211">@kk2211</a></li>
<li>Reranker support - cohere, zeroentropy, huggingface, sentence transformers and LLMs by <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/parshvadaftari/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/parshvadaftari">@parshvadaftari</a></li>
<li>Added metadata filtering for the OSS <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/parshvadaftari/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/parshvadaftari">@parshvadaftari</a></li>
<li>Added Assisstant memory retrieval by <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/parshvadaftari/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/parshvadaftari">@parshvadaftari</a></li>
<li>Improved prompt for better memory retrieval by <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/parshvadaftari/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/parshvadaftari">@parshvadaftari</a></li>
</ul>
<h2> Improvements &amp; Fixes</h2>
<ul>
<li>Refactored <strong>v2 search and update examples</strong> by <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/parshvadaftari/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/parshvadaftari">@parshvadaftari</a></li>
<li>Fixed <strong>Databricks Vector Store</strong> integration by <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/hayescode/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/hayescode">@hayescode</a></li>
<li>Fixed <strong>Milvus DB bug</strong> and added test coverage by <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/parshvadaftari/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/parshvadaftari">@parshvadaftari</a></li>
<li>Fixed <strong>Weaviate search method</strong> by <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/matanco1/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/matanco1">@matanco1</a></li>
<li>Fixed <strong>non-serializable objects</strong> in config deepcopy by <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/lsvishaal/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/lsvishaal">@lsvishaal</a></li>
<li>Fixed <strong>bug with thinking LLM</strong> in vLLM by <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/dog-last/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/dog-last">@dog-last</a></li>
<li>Fixed <strong>license and README metadata</strong> by <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/lsvishaal/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/lsvishaal">@lsvishaal</a></li>
<li>Fixed <strong>hardcoded embedding dimensions</strong> and <strong>TypeScript build issues</strong> by <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/Mrinank-Bhowmick/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/Mrinank-Bhowmick">@Mrinank-Bhowmick</a></li>
<li>Fixed <strong>missing data key</strong> handling during search operations by <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/lsvishaal/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/lsvishaal">@lsvishaal</a></li>
<li>Improved <strong>Get Memories playground</strong> and documentation examples by <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/parshvadaftari/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/parshvadaftari">@parshvadaftari</a></li>
<li>Added <strong>detailed explanation</strong> for <code>output_format v1.1</code> parameter by <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/lsvishaal/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/lsvishaal">@lsvishaal</a></li>
<li>Updated <strong>dependency compatibility</strong> with OpenAI 2.x by <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/yashikabadaya/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/yashikabadaya">@yashikabadaya</a></li>
<li>Updated <strong>main script and removed stale code</strong> by <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/deshraj/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/deshraj">@deshraj</a></li>
<li>Added <strong>version=v2 as default param</strong> in AI SDK <code>add</code> calls by <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/whysosaket/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/whysosaket">@whysosaket</a></li>
<li>Validated <strong>embedding_dims</strong> for Kuzu integration by <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/soapun/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/soapun">@soapun</a></li>
</ul>

        <div data-pjax="true" data-test-selector="body-content" data-view-component="true" class="markdown-body my-3"><h2> What's New in Beta</h2>
<p>This beta release introduces significant improvements to Mem0's core functionality, enhanced vector store integrations, and better LLM provider support.</p>
<h2>New Feature</h2>
<ul>
<li>Added Memgraph compatibility across different versions by <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/parshvadaftari/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/parshvadaftari">@parshvadaftari</a></li>
<li>Added Assisstant memory retrieval by <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/parshvadaftari/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/parshvadaftari">@parshvadaftari</a></li>
<li>Improved prompt for better memory retrieval by <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/parshvadaftari/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/parshvadaftari">@parshvadaftari</a></li>
<li>Reranker support - cohere, zeroentropy, huggingface, sentence transformers and LLMs by <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/parshvadaftari/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/parshvadaftari">@parshvadaftari</a></li>
<li>Add GCP auth for better service account support by <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/parshvadaftari/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/parshvadaftari">@parshvadaftari</a></li>
<li>Added metadata filtering for the OSS <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/parshvadaftari/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/parshvadaftari">@parshvadaftari</a></li>
</ul>
<h2>What's Changed</h2>
<ul>
<li>feat: Add metadata param to TS-SDK in client.update by <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/whysosaket/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/whysosaket">@whysosaket</a> in <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="3381406695" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/mem0ai/mem0/issues/3415" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/mem0ai/mem0/pull/3415/hovercard" href="https://github.com/mem0ai/mem0/pull/3415">#3415</a></li>
<li>fix: Use ConfigDict instead of class-based Config by <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/gabe-l-hart/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/gabe-l-hart">@gabe-l-hart</a> in <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="3379818701" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/mem0ai/mem0/issues/3409" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/mem0ai/mem0/pull/3409/hovercard" href="https://github.com/mem0ai/mem0/pull/3409">#3409</a></li>
<li>databricks bug fixes by <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/hayescode/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/hayescode">@hayescode</a> in <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="3381504281" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/mem0ai/mem0/issues/3416" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/mem0ai/mem0/pull/3416/hovercard" href="https://github.com/mem0ai/mem0/pull/3416">#3416</a></li>

  <h2 class="sr-only" id="hd-7d49fc7e">v0.1.115</h2>

  <div class="d-flex flex-column flex-md-row my-5 flex-justify-center">
